<tr><td width="742"><h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/25/1/1/n14403626.md#1" target="_blank">诗歌：辞旧迎新颂神韵</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/1992513/djy/blob/master/gb/25/1/1/n14403626.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2024/03/id14205594-shutterstock_1706227852-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>神韵圣诞喜迎新，盛况空前颂赞频。
